***necrose.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:necrose.html>necrose</a> (102547)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">necrōsis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νέκρωσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nékrōsis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:necrose.html>necrose</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:necrose.html>necroses</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:necrose.html>necrosetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>necrosis, localized death of cells or living tissue</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nederlaag.html>nederlaag</a> (9037)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nederlaghe</i> (15th c.), probably after early modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Niederlage</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">niderlāge</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the act of sinking to the ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Analysable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neder.html>neder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nether, down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laag.html>laag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">layer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, though the latter word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in the obsolete sense of “act or way of lying” (for which now <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ligging.html>ligging</a></i>).

***nee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a> (55)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>neen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nēn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">none, not one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ne</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">no</span>
<ul><li><b>1992</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A._F._Th._van_der_Heijden" class="extiw" title="w:A. F. Th. van der Heijden">A. F. Th. <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Heijden</a>, <i>Weerborstels</i>, Em. Querido's <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a>, page 23:
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stemming.html>stemming</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a> in.
<dl><dd><b>No</b>, the atmosphere <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> great.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used to show disagreement or negation.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergist.html>vergist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a>.</i>: No, you are mistaken.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mag.html>mag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:televisie.html>televisie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a></i>: No, you may not watch television now.</dd></dl></li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>Nee</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an alternative form, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>neen</a></i>. In Belgium, it functions as a stressed variant of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a></i>. In the Netherlands, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an archaic, formal form in <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> language, but <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> quite common in written language until recently.</li></ul>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>neen</a></li></ul>

<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ontkennen.html>ontkennen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ontkenning.html>ontkenning</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:nietes.html>nietes</a></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nēve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nefo</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nevo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nefô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*népōts</i>.

***neen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>neen</a> (2724)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>neen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nēn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">none, not one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ne</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ne</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:nein.html>nein</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>neen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">no</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">stressed or formal form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nee.html>nee</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>Neen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the stressed form productively used in Flanders in both <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> and written language. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> archaic in both the <a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> as well as written language in the Netherlands.
</p>
</body> 
***neer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a> (498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>down, downwards</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijwoord.html>Bijwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a></b>
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:nederdalen.html>nederdalen</a></i>. "<a href = vnd.unilang:helaas.html>Helaas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> aardgasbaten <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nauwelijks.html>nauwelijks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruikt.html>gebruikt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zorg.html>zorg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dragen.html>dragen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alternatieve.html>alternatieve</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:energiebron.html>energiebronnen</a>, of <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuwe.html>nieuwe</a> verdiencapaciteit <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bouwen.html>bouwen</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>Onze</a> beleidsmakers <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herhaaldelijk.html>herhaaldelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:probleem.html>probleem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewezen.html>gewezen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gekozen.html>gekozen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fundamentele.html>fundamentele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koerswijziging.html>koerswijziging</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***neergooien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:neergooien.html>neergooien</a> (59942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gooien.html>gooien</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neergooien.html>neergooien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cast, throw down, floor</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:neergooien.html>neergooien</a></b> <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>

<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:overgankelijk.html>overgankelijk</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onzorgvuldig.html>onzorgvuldige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wijze.html>wijze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:smijten.html>smijten</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:neerploffen.html>neerploffen</a> (102526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">down</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ploffen.html>ploffen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thud, burst</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neerploffen.html>neerploffen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to let oneself fall or drop suddenly into a resting position
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwam.html>kwam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:binnen.html>binnen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:groette.html>groette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niemand.html>niemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:plofte.html>plofte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> bank.</i>
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> in, didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> hello to anybody and <b>dropped</b> onto the couch.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:neerploffen.html>neerploffen</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:neerslaan.html>neerslaan</a> (19813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slaan.html>slaan</a></i>.

<ol><li>to fall down</li>
<li>to knock down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to precipitate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to condense</li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***negen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:negen.html>negen</a> (1111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">nēgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nigun</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*newun</i>, reflecting earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*newunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁néwn̥</i>, with <i>-t</i> added through influence of "ten".
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negen.html>negen</a></strong> (<i>invariable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>nine</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>A nine, an instance or representation of the digit nine

***negentien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:negentien.html>negentien</a> (7490)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">neghentien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*niguntēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*niguntien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*newuntehun</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">njoggentjin</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">neunzehn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nineteen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">nitten</i>.
</p>

***neger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:neger.html>neger</a> (3493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">negro</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">nègre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">negro</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">niger</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin but possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nókʷts</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">night</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neger.html>neger</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negers.html>negers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negertje.html>negertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negerin.html>negerin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a black person, a Negro <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">male or of unspecified gender</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span></h4>
<ul><li>For many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> in Belgium and the Netherlands it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a neutral and non-offensive way to refer to someone with a darker skin colour. In recent years under influence of the offensiveness of the etymologically related English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nigger</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Negro</i>, some <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> do take offence, making it a topic of some debate whether the word can still be used neutrally or not, with varying opinions being <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a>.</li>
<li>In Suriname, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a derogatory term, except when used in the compounds <i><span class="Latn" lang="nl">bosneger</span></i> and <i><span class="Latn" lang="nl">stadsneger</span></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>
<li>The synonym <i><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zwarte.html>zwarte</a></span></i> can be used as a neutral alternative in all geographies and circumstances.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:negeren.html>negeren</a> (3271)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">negō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I deny</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; the shift in meaning from <i>deny</i> to <i>ignore</i> dates to the second <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> of the 19th century.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negeren.html>negeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ignore <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:negeert.html>negeert</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aantal.html>aantal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagen.html>dagen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> ignoring</b> her for a number of days.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neger.html>neger</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negeren.html>negeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now potentially  offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to belittle, to torment, to treat like a flunky <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***negerin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:negerin.html>negerin</a> (29172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neger.html>neger</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-in</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negerin.html>negerin</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negerinnen.html>negerinnen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:negerinnetje.html>negerinnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">potentially  offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> black woman, negress</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Somewhat more likely to be offensive than <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neger.html>neger</a></i>, which see for <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a> on use.
</p>
